## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph Helm_Source
        ECR[ECR: 519940785508.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com]
        Chart[argocd-app-manager:0.4.3]
        Values1[values.yaml]
        Values2[values.dev1.yaml]
        Param[atomic=true]
    end
    
    subgraph GitLab_Source
        Repo[devops.git]
        Branch[ticket/NF-7629-ingress-4]
    end
    
    subgraph Deployment
        K8s[Kubernetes: argocd namespace]
        App[dev1-app-manager]
    end
    
    ECR --> Chart
    Chart --> Values1
    Chart --> Values2
    Chart --> Param
    Repo --> Branch
    Branch -.provides values.-> Values2
    Chart --> App
    App --> K8s
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Syncing
    Syncing --> Healthy: Deployment Success
    Syncing --> OutOfSync: Drift Detected
    Healthy --> OutOfSync: Manual Change
    OutOfSync --> Syncing: Auto Self-Heal
    Healthy --> [*]
    
    state Syncing {
        [*] --> FetchChart
        FetchChart --> MergeValues
        MergeValues --> ApplyManifests
        ApplyManifests --> [*]
    }
```
